<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="English">English</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=fruit&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: English">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; font-size: 90%; background: #f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">English <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia" title="Wikipedia">Wikipedia</a> has an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/fruit" class="extiw" title="w:fruit">fruit</a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/fruit" class="extiw" title="w:fruit">Wikipedia </a></span></div>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; font-size: 90%; background: #f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">English <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia" title="Wikipedia">Wikipedia</a> has an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fruit_(disambiguation)" class="extiw" title="w:Fruit (disambiguation)">Fruit (disambiguation)</a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fruit_(disambiguation)" class="extiw" title="w:Fruit (disambiguation)">Wikipedia </a></span></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=fruit&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/frute#Middle_English" title="frute">frute</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/fruit#Middle_English" title="fruit">fruit</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/fruct#Middle_English" title="fruct">fruct</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/fruyt#Middle_English" title="fruyt">fruyt</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/frut#Middle_English" title="frut">frut</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fruits and vegetables</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href="/wiki/fruit#Old_French" title="fruit">fruit</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">produce, fruits and vegetables</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/fructus#Latin" title="fructus">fructus</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">enjoyment, proceeds, profits, produce, income</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/frux#Latin" title="frux">frūx</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">crop, produce, fruit</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/fruor#Latin" title="fruor">fruor</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">have the benefit of, to use, to enjoy</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/b%CA%B0ruHg-" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/bʰruHg-">*bʰruHg-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to make use of, to have enjoyment of</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/brook#English" title="brook">brook</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to bear, tolerate</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href="/wiki/brauchen#German" title="brauchen">brauchen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to need</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Displaced native <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/ovet#Middle_English" title="ovet">ovet</a></i> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">"fruit", from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href="/wiki/ofett#Old_English" title="ofett">ofett</a></i>; see <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/ovest#English" title="ovest">ovest</a></i></span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/wastum#Middle_English" title="wastum">wastom, wastum</a></i> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">"fruit, growth", from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href="/wiki/w%C3%A6stm#Old_English" title="wæstm">wæstm</a></i></span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>, and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/blede#Middle_English" title="blede">blede</a></i> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">"fruit, flower, offspring", from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href="/wiki/bled#Old_English" title="bled">blēd</a></i>; see <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/blead#English" title="blead">blead</a></i></span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>.
</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=fruit&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Received_Pronunciation" class="extiw" title="w:Received Pronunciation">Received Pronunciation</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">enPR</a>: <span class="AHD enPR">fro͞ot</span>, <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>:&#32;<span class="IPA">/fɹuːt/</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/General_American" class="extiw" title="w:General American">General American</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>:&#32;<span class="IPA">/fɹut/</span></li>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=fruit&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">fruit</strong> (<i><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#countable" title="Appendix:Glossary">countable</a> and <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#uncountable" title="Appendix:Glossary">uncountable</a></i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/fruits#English" title="fruits">fruits</a></b>) (<i>see <a href="#Usage_notes">Usage notes</a> for discussion of plural</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">often&#32;in the <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#plural" title="Appendix:Glossary">plural</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="use-with-mention">In general,</span> a product of plant growth useful to man or animals.</li>
<li><span class="use-with-mention">Specifically,</span> a sweet, edible part of a plant that resembles seed-bearing fruit <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">see next sense</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, even if it does not develop from a floral ovary; <span class="use-with-mention">also used in a technically imprecise sense for some sweet or sweetish <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/vegetable#English" title="vegetable">vegetables</a></span>, such as the <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/petiole#English" title="petiole">petioles</a></span> of <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/rhubarb#English" title="rhubarb">rhubarb</a></span>, that resemble a true fruit or are used in cookery as if they were a fruit.</span></li></ol>

</td></tr></tbody></table></div><p><span id="attentionseekingen" class="attentionseeking" lang="en" title="see Tea room discussion"></span>
</p><ol><li><ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source">[<b>1930</b>,  “fruit”, in W. T. Harris; F. Sturges Allen, editors, <cite>Webster's New International Dictionary of the English Language Based on the International Dictionary of 1890 and 1900.<span class="q-hellip-sp">&#32;</span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">[</span></span>…<span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">]</span></span><span class="q-hellip-b">&#32;</span></cite>, Springfield, Mass.&#58; G. &amp; C. Merriam, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://hdl.handle.net/2027/uiuo.ark:/13960/t3227430k?urlappend=%3Bseq=1024">pages 872–873</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">In popular usage there is no exact distinction between a <b>fruit</b> and a vegetable, except where the latter consists of the stem, leaves, or root of the plant. Thus the apple, pear, orange, lemon, peach, plum, grape, banana, persimmon, pineapple, and most berries are generally recognized as <b>fruits</b>; the pea, bean, pumpkin, squash, eggplant, cucumber, etc., are vegetables; while the tomato and melon are variously regarded. In general it may be said that a <b>fruit</b> is more frequently eaten in the raw state as a dessert; that it possesses a characteristic aroma and flavor, due to the presence of various organicesters, and when cooked requires sugar to counteract its acidity. <b>Fruit</b> is occasionally applied to certain other vegetable structures of pronounced flavor eaten as a sauce or dessert, as the stalks of rhubarb.</span>]</div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/botany" title="botany">botany</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A product of fertilization in a plant, <span class="use-with-mention">specifically:</span>
<ol><li>The <a href="/wiki/seed" title="seed">seed</a>-bearing part of a plant, often <a href="/wiki/edible" title="edible">edible</a>, colourful and fragrant, produced from a floral <a href="/wiki/ovary" title="ovary">ovary</a> after fertilization.</li>
<li>The spores of <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/cryptogams#English" title="cryptogams">cryptogams</a></span> and their accessory organs.</li></ol>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1640</b>,  John Parkinson,  <cite>Theatrum botanicum: the Theater of Plants; or, An Herball of a Large Extent</cite>, London, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://hdl.handle.net/2027/ucm.5326186323?urlappend=%3Bseq=195">page 1063</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">[A]fter the flower is past commeth the <b>fruit</b> in long pods, every seede bunching out like the pods of Orobus and as bigge almost as the smaller Pease.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>An end result, effect, or consequence; <a href="/wiki/advantageous" title="advantageous">advantageous</a> or <a href="/wiki/disadvantageous" title="disadvantageous">disadvantageous</a> <a href="/wiki/result" title="result">result</a>.
<dl><dd><i>His long nights in the office eventually bore <b>fruit</b> when his business boomed and he was given a raise.</i></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><i><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#c." title="Appendix:Glossary"><abbr title="circa">c.</abbr></a></i> <b>1593</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="w:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>,  “<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Richard_III_(play)" class="extiw" title="w:Richard III (play)">The Tragedy of Richard the Third:<span class="q-hellip-sp">&#160;</span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">[</span></span><span title="With the Landing of Earle Richmond, and the Battel at Bosworth Field.">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">]</span></span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span></a>”, in  <cite>Mr. William Shakespeares Comedies, Histories, &amp; Tragedies: Published According to the True Originall Copies</cite> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/First_Folio" class="extiw" title="w:First Folio">First Folio</a>), London&#58; Printed by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Jaggard" class="extiw" title="w:William Jaggard">Isaac Iaggard</a>, and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edward_Blount" class="extiw" title="w:Edward Blount">Ed[ward] Blount</a>, published 1623, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/606515358">606515358</a></small>, [Act II, scene i]:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">the <b>fruit</b> of rashness</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li>Bible, Isaiah iii. 10
<dl><dd>They shall eat the <b>fruit</b> of their doings.</dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: #777777;">(Can we <a href="/wiki/Category:Requests_for_date" title="Category:Requests for date">date</a> this quote by Macaulay and provide title, author's full name, and other details?)</span>
<dl><dd>The <b>fruits</b> of this education became visible.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_nouns#Attributive" title="Appendix:English nouns">attributive</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Of, belonging to, related to, or having fruit or its characteristics; <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of living things</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> producing or consuming fruit.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">the fresh-squeezed <b>fruit</b> juice; a <b>fruit</b> salad; an artificial <b>fruit</b> flavor; a <b>fruit</b> tree; a <b>fruit</b> bat</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#dated" title="Appendix:Glossary">dated</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span>&#32;<a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#colloquial" title="Appendix:Glossary">colloquial</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span>&#32;<a href="/wiki/derogatory" title="derogatory">derogatory</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href="/wiki/homosexual" title="homosexual">homosexual</a> <a href="/wiki/man" title="man">man</a>; <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/derogatory" title="derogatory">derogatory</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span>&#32;<a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#figurative" title="Appendix:Glossary">figuratively</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> an <a href="/wiki/effeminate" title="effeminate">effeminate</a> <a href="/wiki/man" title="man">man</a>. <span class="defdate">[1900]</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#archaic" title="Appendix:Glossary">archaic</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/offspring" title="offspring">Offspring</a> from a sexual union.
<dl><dd><i>Blessed art thou amongst women and blessed is the <b>fruit</b> of thy womb.</i></dd>
<dd><i>The litter was the <b>fruit</b> of the union between our whippet and their terrier.</i></dd></dl>
<ul><li><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: #777777;">(Can we <a href="/wiki/Category:Requests_for_date" title="Category:Requests for date">date</a> this quote by Shakespeare and provide title, author's full name, and other details?)</span>
<dl><dd>King Edward's <b>fruit</b>, true heir to the English crown</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=fruit&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Usage notes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul><li>In the botanical and figurative senses, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">fruit</i> is usually treated as uncountable:
<dl><dd><i>a bowl of <b>fruit</b></i>; <i>eat plenty of <b>fruit</b></i>; <i>the tree provides <b>fruit</b>.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li><i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/fruits#English" title="fruits">fruits</a></i> is also sometimes used as the plural in the botanical sense:
<dl><dd><i>berries, achenes, and nuts are all <b>fruits</b></i>; <i>the <b>fruits</b> of this plant split into two parts.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li>When <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">fruit</i> is treated as uncountable in the botanical sense, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">a piece of fruit</i> is often used as a <a href="/wiki/singulative" title="singulative">singulative</a>.</li>
<li>In senses other than the botanical or figurative ones derived from the botanical sense, the plural is <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/fruits#English" title="fruits">fruits</a></i>.</li>
<li>The culinary sense often does not cover true fruits that are savoury or used chiefly in savoury foods, such as <a href="/wiki/tomato" title="tomato">tomatoes</a> and <a href="/wiki/pea" title="pea">peas</a>. These are normally described simply as <a href="/wiki/vegetable" title="vegetable">vegetables</a>.</li></ul>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=fruit&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Verb">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">fruit</strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3&#124;s&#124;pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/fruits#English" title="fruits">fruits</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres&#124;ptcp-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/fruiting#English" title="fruiting">fruiting</a></b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past&#124;and&#124;past&#124;ptcp-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/fruited#English" title="fruited">fruited</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To <a href="/wiki/produce" title="produce">produce</a> fruit, seeds, or spores.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1910</b>,  Canada Experimental Farms Service,  <cite>Report of the Dominion Experimental Farms</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">It may be said, however, that the percentage of green apples among the Fameuse seedlings is much less than among the others as out of 33 Fameuse seedlings which had <b>fruited</b> up to this year, none was green and we recollect but one light coloured Fameuse seedling <b>fruiting</b> this year.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1998</b>,  Randy Molina &amp; David Pilz,  <cite>Managing Forest Ecosystems to Conserve Fungus Diversity and Sustain Wild Mushroom Harvests</cite>, <small><a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/0788143433" title="Special:BookSources/0788143433">→ISBN</a></small>, page 10:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">For example, chanterelles and russulas can start <b>fruiting</b> in early to mid summer given sufficient moisture, but other species, such as matsutake, rarely <b>fruit</b> until temperatures cool in the autumn, even if moisture is available earlier.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2014</b>,  David Mitchell,  <cite>The Bone Clocks</cite>, <small><a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/9780340921609" title="Special:BookSources/9780340921609">→ISBN</a></small>, page 12:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">The grass and weeds come up to my waist and the plum trees are already <b>fruiting</b> up, though most of the fruit'll go to the wasps and the worms, Vinny says, 'cause he can't be arsed to pick it.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Dutch">Dutch</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=fruit&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Dutch">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=fruit&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="French">French</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=fruit&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: French">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=fruit&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm"><a href="/wiki/fruict#Middle_French" title="fruict">fruict</a></i>, alteration of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href="/wiki/fruit#Old_French" title="fruit">fruit</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/fructus#Latin" title="fructus">frūctus</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">enjoyment, proceeds, profits, produce, income</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a derivative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/fruor#Latin" title="fruor">fruor</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">have the benefit of, to use, to enjoy</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/b%CA%B0rug-&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/bʰrug- (page does not exist)">*bʰrug-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to make use of, to have enjoyment of</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_6">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=fruit&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="fro">fruit</strong>&#160;<span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>oblique plural</i> <b class="Latn" lang="fro"><a href="/wiki/fruiz#Old_French" title="fruiz">fruiz</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn" lang="fro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=fruitz&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="fruitz (page does not exist)">fruitz</a></b>, <i>nominative singular</i> <b class="Latn" lang="fro"><a href="/wiki/fruiz#Old_French" title="fruiz">fruiz</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn" lang="fro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=fruitz&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="fruitz (page does not exist)">fruitz</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Latn" lang="fro"><strong class="selflink">fruit</strong></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href="#English">fruit</a>
<ul><li><b>circa 1170</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Christian_of_Troyes" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Christian of Troyes">Christian of Troyes</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/fr:%C3%89rec_et_%C3%89nide" class="extiw" title="s:fr:Érec et Énide">Érec et Énide</a></i>
